#Browse this section to know about egress and ingress policies in Foundry

---

# Egress Policy Guidelines

Palantir Foundry is hosted on the Palantir Cloud (PCloud) and is accessed via the internet. To establish a data connection between PCloud and an external network or application, please refer to the guidelines provided below.

## PCloud to Merck
If your system is an internal Merck system on-premise or Merck-owned AWS environment with Data Center Extension("MCloud"):
-	Check if your server or application can access Palantir Foundry: [https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/) by opening a browser. 
In case its not working
-	Check any Firewall blocks with the IT -> Open an Firewall request with IT
-	Check if the Merck Root CA certificate is installed in the CA Certification Keystore that your java installation is using -> If not work with IT to provide the certificate


## PCloud to Cloud

If an outbound connection from Foundry is required for another external system the following applies:
1)	The person requiring the access shall open a service request and provide the following information:
-	User ID (e.g. M123456)
-	Business Sector (Sector Data Office, SDO) 
-	Details about the source to access
-	Domain names/IPs + ports that require allowlisting (FQDN or IP)
-	Business justification for this request
Label the issue with the "Inquiry Type: Network changes"

2)	An Operations Team member shall involve the SDO/MDAO lead architects ("SDO Admins" group in Foundry). Two of the lead architects shall give approval to create the egress policy.

3)	If the public IP is from China then Foundry Support/PCS needs to be added to the ticket for whitelisting. If not, the egress policy is created in the Foundry Control Panel by a lead architect. 
à By default, egress policies shall link the service request that requested this policy in the description. Also the policy should not be a global policy and permissions should be granted on request basis

4)	Once done, service request shall be updated and closed after successful testing. 

The below option needs to be enabled in the "Code import configuration" section of the Data Connection source to consume egress policies in the project:

![](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/workbenches/egress_policy.png)

---

# Ingress Policy Guidelines

For general inbound connections from Merck IP ranges listed on [verkehrsnachrichten.merck.de/inet/Public-IPINFO.txt](https://verkehrsnachrichten.merck.de/inet/Public-IPINFO.txt) , the Operations Team will be notified by the Network Team through the Outlook Distribution List (iap-update@merckgroup.com). Upon receiving this notification, an Operations Team member will create a service request, attaching the notification email and including an MDAO lead architect, along with a link to the ingress change request in the Control Panel to approve it.

If an inbound connection to Foundry is required for any external service outside the standard Merck IP ranges and only if it is a Single-Tenant, fully dedicated Merck IP-owned system(Multi-Tenant systems will not be allowlisted), then a more detailed review is required -

1)	The person requiring the access shall open a ticket and provide the following information:
-	User ID (e.g. M123456)
-	Business Sector (Sector Data Office, SDO) 
-	Details about the system that requires access to Foundry
-	IPs that require allowlisting
-	Business justification for this request
Label the issue with the "Inquiry Type: Network changes"

2)	An Operations Team member will include Nicolas Renkamp / Andrew McArdle / Dominik Schneider in the ticket for allowlisting.
3)	If approved, the Operations team creates an ingress change request in Control Panel and shares the link with lead architect in the ticket for approval.

4)	Once done, the ticket shall be updated and closed after successful testing.

# Architecture & Component Overview

The following pages include high level information about UPTIMIZE Foundry.

---

# <span style="color:#0F69AF"> Development Tool Framework</span>



Welcome to our Development Tool Framework! We have created a quick guide for you to find out which tools will support you on your analytics journey. Scroll down and discover what's out there or watch [this video](https://web.microsoftstream.com/video/694c60e3-175c-45ac-9301-2a888b3b7a41?channelId=f8e53e68-4025-4654-8f3b-b063ba1d882b) (provided by Life Science ACE) for a deep-dive on the framework.

Ann, Lucas and Matt all work with data. But which development tools for Data Visualization, Data Capture & Acquisition and Data Integration & Modeling are the right ones for their specific needs?

<img src="https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/ArchitectureComponent_Overview/Devlopment_tool_Framework/three_boxes.png" style="width:700px;"/>

# <span style="color:#0F69AF">Tool Descriptions:</span>

||| 
|:--|:--|
| <span style="color:#0F69AF">**Notepad:**</span> Notepad is a collaborative rich-text editor with object integration and template creation features ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/notepad) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/notepad/overview))|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Hubble / object explorer:**</span> Point and click solution to explore your data objects and relations between them through interactive charts ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/hubble) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/object-explorer/overview))
| <span style="color:#0F69AF">**Contour:**</span> User friendly, intuitive point & click tool for quick top-down analysis of large data ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/splash/contour-app) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/contour/overview))|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Workshop:**</span> Create high-quality, easy-to-maintain operational applications using native object components in a point-and-click environment ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/splash/module) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/workshop/overview))
| <span style="color:#0F69AF">**Tableau:**</span> Analyze your data and build out-of-box interactive analytic visuals (dashboards, reports, story) via drag-and-drop and share ([open app](https://mtableau.merckgroup.com/) & [read documentation](https://mdigital.sharepoint.com/sites/Tableau_Knowledge_Base/SitePages/All-about-Tableau.aspx))|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Code workbook:**</span> Visualization support to create detailed, interactive images with commonly used packages (Matplotlib, Plotly, Seaborn) ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/splash/vector) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/code-workbook/overview))
| <span style="color:#0F69AF">**Slate:**</span> Build elaborate sophisticated apps that query and analyze data with drag-and-drop visualization and input widgets to drive business workflows ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/slate/create) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/slate/overview))|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Code repository:**</span> Enhance object ontology functions & relations e.g. for use in workshop dashboards (in TypeScript) ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/splash/code) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/code-repositories/overview))
| <span style="color:#0F69AF">**Map:**</span> Analyze geospatial data ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/vortex)) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/map/overview)|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Code Workspace:**</span> Code Workspace integrates JupyterLab® and RStudio® Workbench into Palantir Foundry, enhancing productivity and data security. ([read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/code-workspaces/overview)) To get access to the Code workspace, please raise an issue in the Foundry Issue app.
|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Vertex:**</span> Explore object graphs ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/vertex) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/vertex/overview))|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Quiver:**</span> Visualize, analyze, and transform Foundry-backed objects and time series at scale ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/splash/quiver) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/quiver/overview))

|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Scheduler:** </span> Enables you to set up scheduled builds of your data pipelines in order to ensure that your data stays up-to-date ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/scheduler/overview) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/data-integration/schedules))|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Pipeline Builder:**</span> Point & click tool for building data integration pipelines from data sources through to final outputs ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/data-integration/builder/) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/pipeline-builder/overview/))
|<span style="color:#0F69AF">**Builds/Job Tracker:**</span> Computes new dataset versions through orchestrated jobs, each defined by shared logic and JobSpecs define how a job should be constructed and are published when data transformation logic changes ([open app](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/data-integration/job-tracker/builds) & [read documentation](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/data-integration/builds))

# Foundry Overview

## Foundry Overview
Foundry enables the storage, management, and discovery of your enterprise data. While users interact with a streamlined front end, Foundry is operating a series of backend services to manage this complexity.

Please follow this [link](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/docs/foundry/getting-started/introductory-concepts) to see the Foundry documentation:

![overview](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/ArchitectureComponent_Overview/Foundry_Overview/palantir_overview.png)

---

# Data Architecture Overview  

The following diagram shows a condensed view of the basic components of a typical data pipeline in Foundry. It includes the four levels of a data pipeline in the middle path (bottom to top) plus Data Treasury and Ontology Management.

![overview](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/ArchitectureComponent_Overview/data_architecture_overview.png)

---

# Pipeline Stages Overview

The following diagram shows the different pipeline stages.

![stages](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/ArchitectureComponent_Overview/Advanced/Pipeline_Stages_Overview/pipeline_stages.png)
Please note that a "workflow" project is considered a "Use Case Project".

## Data Connections

Through the data connection, raw data from source systems lands into a Data source Project.  
*Responsibility:* Sector Data Office

## Data Source Project

A single Data source Project, per logical data source, defines the basic cleanup steps for each raw dataset and applies a consistent schema.  
*Responsibility:* Sector Data Office

## Transform Project

Datasets are imported from one or more Data source Projects and transformed to produce canonical, re-usable datasets.  
*Responsibility:* Sector Data Office; any other user can work there under SDO governance

## Ontology Project

Datasets are imported from one or more Transform Projects and transformed to produce the canonical tables representing discrete data treasury items. A single Ontology Project often groups related sets of data for a given business domain for ease of management. In the usual case, ontology datasets are published in data treasury and that the schema and semantics of ontology datasets provide a contract to the data consumer. This contract can only be changed in a forward compatible way.  
*Responsibility:* Sector Data Office; any other user can work there under SDO governance

## Use Case Project

Use case projects import data from ontology projects to pursue a specific outcome. Frequently this is an operation workflow, data science investigation, business intelligence analysis and report, or application development project.  
*Responsibility:* Use Cases can be self-serve or SDO-driven.

The below diagram shows the complete end-to-end pipeline & included components of a standard data pipeline from data source to potential exposure to 3rd party downstream applications. It includes the mandatory standard path and optional artifacts (dotted).

![pipeline](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/ArchitectureComponent_Overview/Advanced/Pipeline_Stages_Overview/end_to_end_pipeline.png)

## Pipeline Responsibility

The following diagram depicts the logical separation of responsibilities of SDO and Business.

![responsibility](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/ArchitectureComponent_Overview/Advanced/Pipeline_Stages_Overview/pipeline_responsibility.png)

# Foundry Access Management

There are access management concepts in <b class="custom-color">UPTIMIZE Foundry</b>  centered around 

* [Use Cases](/foundry/access-management/use-case/),
* [Data Treasury Items](/foundry/access-management/dti/)
* [Data Source and Transform projects](foundry/access-management/data-source-transform/)
* [Wrapper or Capability groups](/foundry/access-management/wrapper-groups/).

There are now options to use 
* [Organization-aligned access management (Entitlements)](foundry/access-management/use-case/organization-aligned-access-management/).
* [Priviledged Entitlements](foundry/access-management/use-case/privileged-entitlement-user-guide/).

## User Access Management Portal

All access requests can be created and managed in the <a href="https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.60d62422-3f90-4bfb-8b5e-b33a4ccd966e/main">Foundry User Access Management App</a>.

<a href="/assets/foundry/foundry-access-portal.png"><img src="/assets/foundry/foundry-access-portal.png" width="100%">



### Request Access


1. Open to the User [Access Management Application](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.60d62422-3f90-4bfb-8b5e-b33a4ccd966e/main)
2. On the top left click on "New Access Request" and select the object you want to request access to. 
3. Once you have filled out all required fields, you can submit the access request.


### View Access Requests: Data Treasury Items & Use Cases

| | |
|:---------|:---------------|
| - Navigate to the [User Access Management](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.60d62422-3f90-4bfb-8b5e-b33a4ccd966e) application. You will find all your access requests under the tab "My access requests". <br><br> - This will show you the access requests you have created. <br><br> - By default the list will show all open access requests. If you want to see your previously raised access requests, click on "All" under the tab "My access requests". <br><br> |![access_request_pending](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/access_request_pending.png) |




### Approve / Reject Access Requests: Data Treasury Items, Use Cases & Source/Transform Projects

| | |
|:---------|:---------------|
| - Navigate to the [User Access Management](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.60d62422-3f90-4bfb-8b5e-b33a4ccd966e) application. You will find the  access requests you can Approve or Reject under the tab "Manage access requests". <br><br> - This will show you the access requests you have to manage by either Approving or Rejecting them. <br><br> - By default the list will show all open access requests. If you want to see your previously raised access requests, click on "All" under the tab "My access requests". <br><br> |![approver_view](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/approver_view.png) |
*Please note that requests to Data Source & Transform projects can only be approved by SDO & MDAO Data Ingestion teams.*

### Revoke Access from Access Requests: Use Cases, Data Treasury Items

The following criteria must be met: 
- Who? Use Case/DTI Owner only.<br>
- The Access Request must be in <b>granted</b><br>

Please note: 
- Revoke User Access is possible only for Use Case Access Requests.<br>
- Entire Request revocation is only possible for both: Use Case and DTI Access Request.<br>

| Type | Action |
|:---------|:---------------|
| <b>Revoke Entire Access - DTI</b><br><br>Navigate to the "Revoke" button and Select the option "Revoke".|![revoke-dti-access-request](/assets/foundry-access-management/revoke-dti-access-request.png) |
| <b>Revoke Entire Access - Use Case</b><br><br>Navigate to the "Revoke" button, Select the option "Revoke Enitre Request" and Submit|![revoke-uc-access-request](/assets/foundry-access-management/revoke-uc-access-request.png) |
| <b>Revoke Individual User Access - Use Case</b><br><br>Navigate to the "Revoke" button<br><br> Select the option "Revoke User Access"<br><br> Select User(s)/Group(s) and Submit |![revoke-individual-user-access](/assets/foundry-access-management/revoke-indivdual-user-access.jpg) |

# Access Management for Use Cases

<b class="custom-color">Access Requests</b> manage permissions for access to use cases, more precisely to the use case's projects.

<a href="/assets/foundry/foundry-request-access.png"><img src="/assets/foundry/foundry-request-access.png" alt="request_access" width="400px"></a>

An access request links:

* One or several users or an Entitlement,
* a request reason

to

* a Use Case
* this Use Case Project(s)
* this Use Case Groups that manage access to the projects.

Access requests may also be only temporary. 

The use case owners, that is the Business Owner, Product Owner or Technical Owner may approve, reject or revoke access requests.



## Use Case Groups

The standard groups for a project are


| Group | Naming Convention | Purpose |
| -- | -- | -- |
| Owner Group | ``<projectname>-owner ``| High-level administrator group. Contains the Business Owner, the Product Owner and the Technical Owner. Not selectable in Access requests. |
| Editor Group | ``<projectname>-editor ``| Project contributors. People who are supposed to build in Foundry.|
| Viewer Group | ``<projectname>-viewer ``| Consumers that can only view the content of a project.|

These groups are automatically created in the use case life cycle process.

Once the Use Case owner grant an access request, users are automatically added to the respective group permitting them the desired level of access.


## Presets

Use case owners may define <b class="custom-color">Presets</b> which are predefined collections of Projects and Groups which allow for a more streamlined access process.

Use Case Owners can define a so called permission preset which is a  combination of a project(s) and a group(s). Each use case owner (Product Owner, Business Owner, Tech Lead) can specify a permission preset in the personal view of the use case portal.

| | |
|:---------|:---------------|
| - Navigate to the personal view of your use case an click on the "More" menu. <br><br> - In this menu you have the option to manage permission presets. <br><br> - To do so, click on "Manage use case permission presets". <br><br> | ![managing_permissions](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/managing_permissions.png) |
| - A new window will appear where you can see existing permission presets, create new permission presets or delete permission presets. <br><br> - To create  a new permission preset, click on "New Permission Preset" <br><br>  | ![permission_preset](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/permission_preset.png)|
| - A form will appear which allows you to define the permission preset for the selected use case. <br><br> - You can specify a name for the permission preset which will then be shown in the users requesting access to your use case. <br><br> - Next you can select the groups which should be part of the permission preset. <br><br> - Finally the form allows you to assign delegates to the permission preset. These delegates can approve access requests only for the specific permission preset. <br><br> - **Please note** that only [compliant groups](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/notepad/view/ri.notepad.main.notepad.011036c1-b4f8-4638-b899-56a8fa474787) and compliant sub-groups can be selected. Sub-groups should be part of a compliant use case group and follow the same naming convention as your use case.  <br><br> + In case a non-compliant group has to be added to a permission preset, please open an [issue](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/issues-app/). This requires approval from the SDO Lead Architect. <br><br> | ![permissions_preset_create](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/permission_preset_create.png)|


## Entitlements
Access to Use Cases support
s **organization-aligned access management**. Access can be granted to individual users or based on predefined **Entitlements** managed in the [EMSS platform](https://entitlement.giam.merckgroup.com/), ensuring that access is assigned dynamically based on the organization's structure.

**Key Features**
- **Entitlement-Based Access:** Users can request access to a Use Case through an Entitlement rather than as individual accounts.
- **Automated Access Updates:** Access is granted or revoked automatically based on entitlement membership.
- **Integration with EMSS:** Scope and entitlement management happens in EMSS, while the UAM portal provides visibility into these configurations.

*For more details on the implementation of organization-Aligned Access in Foundry, refer to [this guide](foundry/access-management/organization-aligned-access-management/)*

![concept_access_request_use_case](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/concept_access_request_use_case.png)

# Request Access to Use Cases

*Please note: the user interface is under constant development, so the screenshots you see below might be changing and will get updated regularly.*

1. If you want to access a particular Use Case, can request access directly in the [Use Case Portal](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.cfbd54d9-5f5e-4c67-a94d-37fc842812cc) (access via the home page or navigation bar).
2. Once you have opened the Use Case Portal, you can then browse through the available Use Cases and select the one you want access to by clicking on the selected item. It will take you to the landing page of that specific Use Case.
3. From here, you can click on the **'Request Permission Access'** button, which will take you to the access request form that needs to be completed to gain the required access:


|  |**Use Case Access Requests Form:**
|:---------|:---------------|
| ![access_request_1](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/Access_Management/Access_Control/uc_access_request_step_1.png) | - You can either access via the [User Access Management](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.60d62422-3f90-4bfb-8b5e-b33a4ccd966e) or the [Use Case Portal](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.cfbd54d9-5f5e-4c67-a94d-37fc842812cc)<br><br> - After selecting the **Use Case** you want access to, choose **how you want to grant access**: <br><br> - **User**: Grants individual access to one or several users. <br><br> - **Entitlement**: Grants access to an Entitlement, selecting this option will ensure that all current and future users assigned to that Entitlement receive requested access. If the required entitlement is not available you can raise an issue to request its creation. |
| ![access_request_2](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/Access_Management/Access_Control/uc_access_request_step_2.png) | - Once selected the access type, you must select the **associated projects and relevant access groups** you want to gain access to. <br><br> - Many Use Cases have only one linked project, but some may have multiple. <br><br> - If you are unsure which project to select, please reach out to the **Use Case Owner** for guidance. <br><br> - **Permission Presets:** Use Case Owners can define presets, which are predefined combinations of projects and groups. If a preset exists, you don't need to manually select any project or group. The preset dropdown will only appear for Use Cases with a predefined permission preset. <br><br> - Once you have selected the Use Case project you want to get access to, you can select a group from the project. |
| ![access_request_3](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/Access_Management/Access_Control/uc_access_request_step_3.png) | - You can choose between the project viewer and editor group. <br><br> + **View** Access: Users can view all the content in the use case project. <br><br> + **Edit** Access: Users can edit all (create, change, delete) contents in the use case project.<br><br> - It is important that a valid reason is provided why you need access to the specific Use Case.<br><br> - If you need access only for a certain period, you can set an expiration date of your access request.<br><br>|

# Organization-Aligned Access Management (Entitlements)

## Introduction

The Organization-Aligned Access Management feature introduces a structured way to grant and manage access to Use Cases through **Scopes** and **Entitlements**.
This approach ensures that users automatically receive and retain the appropriate level of access based on their **department**, **role**, and **organizational alignment**.

This functionality is powered by the entitlement management technology implemented in **EMSS** and integrates seamlessly with our system.
By leveraging this technology, we ensure:

- **Centralized access management** across multiple applications.
- **Consistent access control** based on organizational structures.
- **Automated permission updates** when users change departments or roles.

For a deeper understanding of how **EMSS** manages entitlements, refer to their [official documentation](https://evarooms.merckgroup.com/Topic/EUS/en-us/services/entitlement-(emss)).

## Workflow Overview

The following diagram illustrates the **Scope and Entitlement Management** flow across different users and systems, including the UAM Portal (Foundry) and the EMSS Platform.

<br>

![Entitlements Sequence Diagram](/assets/foundry-access-management/entitlements_workflow.png)

**Permissions**

Different actions within the platform are restricted based on user roles:

| Action                             | Who Can Perform It          |
| -------------------------------- | -------------------------------- |
| Create and Import Scopes | SDAOs Only |
| Manage Scopes & Entitlements | SDAOs and their assigned delegates |
| Request Entitlement Access to Use Cases | Any Foundry User |
| Approve/Reject Entitlement Access Requests | Use Case Owners |

**What are the privileged groups of the SDAOs?**

SDAOs are members of one of the following groups:
- [hc-hdd-data-governance](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/settings/groups/3c917b4b-60f0-4b38-b7d1-4dcc8115b8ee) (Healthcare) 
- [ls-ace-platform-admins](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/settings/groups/f9a68fa8-68d3-4479-87fa-830ac4bfe57a) (Life Science)
- [el-governance-team](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/settings/groups/66efb2d6-804c-42aa-af8b-240368a9bf54) (Electronics)
- [mgf-enablement-experts](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/settings/groups/e2a47307-7c81-4a0e-bbb3-34fbf7a9594b) (Group Functions)


**1. Scope Creation**
- The **SDAO** initiates the Scope creation via an action form in the **UAM Portal**.
- A webhook triggers the creation of the Scope in the **EMSS Platform**.
- The **EMSS Platform** confirms the creation.
- A link to the Scope in **EMSS** is provided.

When creating a Scope, the Owner can assign **Delegates** -- secondary contacts who share the same permissions as the Owner.
Delegates can be either internal or external users, ensuring flexibility in Scope management. **At least one** delegate must be assigned to a Scope.

**Scopes should be named using the format** "**[Sector] [Purpose]**" (e.g., "MDAO Governance"). This keeps naming clear, consistent, and easy to navigate.

![Create Scope Action](/assets/foundry-access-management/create_scope.png)

**2. Scope Import**
- The **SDAO** initiates the Scope import via an action form in the **UAM Portal**.
- A Scope Object with the provided ID is created in **Foundry**.
- The Scope will remain in status *WAITING SYNC* until its data is fetched.

![Import Scope Action](/assets/foundry-access-management/import_scope.png)

**3. Managing Scopes and Entitlements**
- The **SDAO** and **delegates** can access the link to the Scope in the EMSS Platform to edit its properties and create/modify its entitlements.
- To maintain consistency with Foundry Users, Entitlements should **include only Primary Accounts** (Internal or External). These can be specified when defining the entitlement.
- Entitlements **must not include** direct user assignments.

![Create Entitlement](/assets/foundry-access-management/create_entitlement.png)

**4. Fetching Data from EMSS**
- Changes made in the EMSS Platform, such as updates to entitlements, are **not immediately reflected** in Foundry.
- A synchronization script runs every **2 hours** to fetch the latest Scope and Entitlement data, ensuring consistency.
- Once synced, the **SDAO** and **Delegates** can visualize the Scope and its associated Entitlements in the **UAM Portal**.

**5. Requesting Use Case Access**
- An **End-User** submits a request for access to a Use Case for a specific Entitlement (or Entitlements) through the **Use Case Portal**.
- A notification is sent to the Use-Case Owner.

![Request Entitlement Access](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Foundry/Access_Management/Access_Control/request_entitlement_access_action_form.png)


For more details on the process of requesting access to a Use Case for an Entitlement, please refer to [this page](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/foundry/foundry-access-management/#request-access%3A-use-cases).

**6. Access Request Approval/Rejection**
- The **Use Case Owner** reviews the request and either approves or rejects it in the UAM Portal.
- If approved, the **multipass-group(s)** associated to the Entitlement(s) is granted access to the Use Case.
- Notifications are sent to the End-User about the outcome.

## Manage Scopes Interface

The new **"Manage Scopes"** tab in the **User Access Management (UAM) portal** allows users to create and manage Scopes.
A Scope serves as a wrapper for multiple Entitlements, grouping them under a single entity for streamlined access management.

From this tab, users can:

- Create new Scopes.
- Import Scopes.
- View existing Scopes along with their details.
- See which Entitlements are associated with each Scope.
- Access the EMSS platform to manage their Scopes.

![UAM Portal](/assets/foundry-access-management/UAM_portal.png)


## Predefined Entitlements in MDAO Governance
The [*MDAO Governance Scope*](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.60d62422-3f90-4bfb-8b5e-b33a4ccd966e/main?scope_id=612854) provides several default entitlements that represent commonly used groups, such as All Members for each sector.
These predefined entitlements simplify access management and ensure consistency across governance processes.


## Interaction between Foundry & EMSS

**Data Sync Method & Frequency**

- **Foundry to EMSS Sync:** The creation of new Scopes in Foundry triggers an automated update in the EMSS system.
- **EMSS to Foundry Sync:** Data from EMSS is synced to Foundry every 2 hours.
- **Impact on Users:** Changes in entitlements are reflected in access permissions automatically.

**Where Actions Are Performed**

| Task                             | Where It's Done                  |
| -------------------------------- | -------------------------------- |
| Create and Import Scopes | Foundry (UAM Portal - Manage Scopes tab) |
| Create and Assign Entitlements to Scopes | EMSS Application |
| Manage individual Entitlements | EMSS Application |
| Request Entitlement Access to Use Cases | Foundry (Use Case Portal) |
| Approve/Reject Entitlement Access Requests | Foundry (User Access Management) |


## Workflow to Create a New Entitlement

The following workflow guides users through the process of requesting a new entitlement. To maintain proper governance and control, **only SDAOs and their designated Delegates** can create entitlements directly. All other users must submit a request through the issue tracking system.

![New Entitlement Workflow](/assets/foundry-access-management/create-new-entitlement-process.png)

### Step-by-Step Process

**Step 1: Check Scope Availability and Permissions**

Navigate to the [*UAM Portal*](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.60d62422-3f90-4bfb-8b5e-b33a4ccd966e/main) and access the **"Entitlements & Scopes"** tab to verify:

- Does the required Scope already exist for your business need?

**Step 2: Choose Your Path**

**✅ If YES** (Scope exists):
- **Raise an issue** via the [*Foundry Issues App*](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/issues-app/), select the **UPTIMIZE Entitlement Request** support type and fulfill the requested information.
- The assigned SDAO or Delegate will review your request and create the entitlement in the [*EMSS Platform*](https://entitlement.giam.merckgroup.com/entitlement/new)
- You will be notified once the entitlement is created and available

**❌ If NO** (Scope doesn't exist):
- Contact your sector's **SDAO** to request:
  - Creation of the required Scope (following the procedure in **Section 1** of the main workflow)
- Once the Scope is created, follow the process above to request your entitlement

# Privileged Entitlement User Access Management

## Overview

The Privileged Entitlement system allows you to request and get access to protected resources such as AWS or Snowflake accounts via their Foundry use cases through a streamlined approval process. This system validates prerequisites, manages approvals, and ensures secure access to critical resources.

## What are Privileged Entitlements?

Privileged Entitlements are a subset of entitlements which are set to get access to specific resources, roles or accounts and that have their own User Access Management process. Unlike other Entitlements, membership to these entitlements can only be obtained through this UAM and resulting multipass groups sync individual accounts as members to Foundry. 

Some characteristics of the system are:
- **Prerequisites validation** (training, accounts, etc.)
- **Approval workflows** from Use Case Owners and Entitlement Delegates
- **Time-limited access** with optional expiration dates
- **Audit trails** for compliance

## Creating an Access Request

Navigate to the [User Access Management App](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.60d62422-3f90-4bfb-8b5e-b33a4ccd966e/main) and click on 'New Access Request' > 'Privileged Entitlements'.

![UAM App](/assets/foundry-access-management/uam-app-privileged-entitlements.png)

Alternatively, go to the Account you are interested in getting access to and click 'Request Access' in this view. Some items, such as the Use Case, Account Type, and Account, will be auto-populated. The standard route to the Account view is: Use Case Portal → Use Case → AWS/Snowflake Extension → Account.".

![AWS Account Request Access](/assets/foundry-access-management/aws-account-request-access.png)

In this view, you can also navigate to the 'Account Entitlements' tab and check the available entitlements for the specific account.

![Account Entitlements](/assets/foundry-access-management/account-entitlements.png)

![Entitlements Focus View From Account Entitlements](/assets/foundry-access-management/entitlement-focus-view-from-account.png)


### Step 1: Fill Out the Request Form

![Create ARO PE Extension Form](/assets/foundry-access-management/create-aro-pe-extension-form.png)

To request access, you'll need to provide:

1. **Use Case**: Select the target use case (AWS Use Case, Snowflake Use Case, etc.)
2. **Account Type**: Select the target account type (AWS, Snowflake)
3. **User Requesting Access**: Specify who needs access (yourself or another user)
4. **Type of ID**: Choose the identity type:
   - **MUID/XUID**: Your Merck/External user id
   - **SADM**: Super Admin Account. **Note**: If you select this option and you don't have an account the action will fail.
5. **Account**: Select the relevant account the entitlement belongs to. You can input the Account ID and the dropdown will filter the results.
6. **Entitlement**: Select the specific entitlement and permission level (e.g., factory_developer, factory_admin)
7. **Reason**: Provide justification for the access request (required for audit)
8. **Expiration Date** (optional): Set a date when access should automatically expire
9. **Auto Approval** (optional): Enable automatic approval if you are also an approver

### Step 2: Submit Your Request

After submitting, the system will:
- Validate that the entitlement is linked to your selected use case
- Route the request to appropriate approvers
- Check your prerequisites (training, required accounts)

While the request is being processed and in status **'pending'** you will be able to access it under the 'My Open Access Requests' section. If is in another status such as 'pre-approved' or 'auto-approved', it will be visible under the 'All My Access Requests' page.

It will also be accessible from the 'Access Requests' tab in the Account View.

The request view will be the following:

![ARO PE View](/assets/foundry-access-management/aro-request-view.png)

## Understanding Request Status

Your request will move through these states:

| Status | Description |
|--------|-------------|
| **pending** | Awaiting approval from Use Case Owner or Entitlement Delegates |
| **auto-approve** | Eligible for automatic approval (you are an approver) |
| **granted** | Access successfully provisioned |
| **granting_failed** | Provisioning failed - contact support |
| **pre-approved** | Pre-approved pending prerequisite completion |
| **revoked** | Access removed |
| **revocation_failed** | Revocation failed - contact support |

## Prerequisites

Before access can be granted, you must complete certain prerequisites based on the resource type and role:

### All AWS Roles
- **Training completion** (mandatory)
- For AWS Factory Admin: HR4You curriculum UP_SAC
- For the rest: HR4You curriculum UP_TEC

> **Note:** Training completion data won't be available until 6:20 AM CET of the next day. If you completed the training today, please wait until tomorrow, then click the "Run Checks" button and the check will pass. If after one day checks are still not passing, please contact AWS Ops Team, they are able to grant access overriding failing checks.

### AWS Factory Admin & Developer Advanced
- **SADM Account** (mandatory)
- Active SADM account must exist and must have been selected to be added to the entitlement, otherwise request creation will fail.

### Snowflake Roles
- At the moment, pre-requisites are not needed

### Prerequisite Status

| Status | Meaning | Can Approve? |
|--------|---------|--------------|
| **COMPLETED** | All mandatory prerequisites passed | ✅ Yes |
| **MISSING_RECOMMENDED** | Only recommended prerequisites missing | ✅ Yes (with risk acknowledgment) |
| **MISSING_MANDATORY** | Mandatory prerequisites incomplete | ❌ No |
| **NOT_REQUIRED** | No prerequisites needed | ✅ Yes |

### Checking Prerequisites

If you've completed missing prerequisites:
1. Click the **"Run Checks"** button on your request
2. The system will verify your updated status
3. If prerequisites are now complete and your request was pre-approved, it will automatically be granted

## Approval Process

### Standard Approval

1. **Approvers**: Use Case Owners and Entitlement Delegates can approve requests
2. **Review**: Approvers see your request details, reason, and prerequisite status
3. **Decision**: Approvers can:
   - **Approve** - Access is immediately provisioned
   - **Reject** - Request is denied with optional feedback
   - **Pre-Approve** - Approve pending prerequisite completion (see below)

### Auto-Approval

Auto-approval happens when:
- You enable the **Auto Approval** option during request creation, AND
- You are also an approver for the resource

**How it works:**
1. Request is created with status `auto-approve`
2. System automatically validates the request
3. Access is provisioned without manual approval
4. You receive confirmation notification

## Pre-Approval Workflow

Pre-approval allows approvers to approve your request before all prerequisites are complete.

### How Pre-Approval Works

1. **Approver Reviews**: Even if prerequisites are incomplete, approvers can click **"Pre-Approve"**
2. **Status Changes**: Your request moves to `PRE_APPROVED` status
3. **Complete Prerequisites**: You complete any missing requirements (training, accounts, etc.)
4. **Automatic Granting**: The next time the **"Run Checks"** action is run on the request, prerequisites are verified and access is automatically provisioned

### Benefits
- Reduces delays in the approval process
- Approvers don't need to review twice
- You can focus on completing prerequisites
- No need to submit a new request

### Process Flow

```
Request Submitted → Pre-Approved → Complete Prerequisites → Auto-Granted ✓
        ↓                              ↓
  (Missing Prerequisites)    (Manual Re-check or Automatic Verification)
```

## Revoking Access

Access can be revoked in several ways:

### Manual Revocation
- Use Case Owners, Entitlement Delegates and AWS Operations team can revoke access at any time
- Click **"Revoke"** on an active access request
- Access is immediately removed from the entitlement

### Automatic Revocation
- If you set an expiration date, access is automatically revoked on that date
- If your prerequisites expire (e.g., training expires), access may be revoked

### Revocation Status
- **revoked**: Access successfully removed
- **revocation_failed**: Revocation failed - contact support for manual intervention

## Managing Entitlement Delegates

Use Case Owners can designate delegates who have the authority to manage access requests on their behalf.

### How to Edit Entitlement Delegates

![Edit Entitlement Delegates](assets/foundry-access-management/edit-entitlement-delegates.png)

1. Navigate to the **Entitlement Object View**
2. Click the **"Edit Entitlement Delegates"** button
3. Add or remove delegates as needed
4. Save your changes

### What Happens When Delegates are Updated

When you modify the entitlement delegates:
- All delegates can approve and revoke access requests as if they were Use Case Owners
- The system automatically updates **all existing access requests** linked to this entitlement
- Updated requests include all statuses **except** rejected and revoked
- New delegates immediately gain approval authority for pending and active requests

### Delegate Permissions

Entitlement Delegates have the same permissions as Use Case Owners:
- Approve access requests
- Reject access requests
- Pre-approve requests pending prerequisites
- Revoke active access
- View all requests for the entitlement

## Notifications

You'll receive notifications for:
- Request submission confirmation
- Prerequisite completion requirements
- Approval or rejection decisions
- Pre-approval status
- Access granted confirmation
- Access revocation notices
- Prerequisite expiration warnings

## Access Request Properties

![ARO PE View](/assets/foundry-access-management/aro-request-view.png)

When viewing your request, you'll see the following information:

### Overview Tab

- **Access Request Title**: Description of the request
- **Created At**: Timestamp when the request was created
- **Created By**: User who created the request
- **User Requesting Access**: The user who will receive access
- **Account to add to Entitlement**: The account identifier (email or SADM ID) that will be added
- **Status**: Current state of the request (pending, granted, revoked, etc.)
- **Approvers**: List of users who can approve this request (owners and delegates)
- **Entitlement Id**: Unique identifier of the entitlement
- **Entitlement Role**: Role associated with the entitlement (e.g., Factory Admin, Developer)
- **Access Request Id**: Unique identifier for this access request
- **Last Prerequisite Check At**: Timestamp of the most recent prerequisite verification
- **Last Prerequisite Check Status**: Current prerequisite status (COMPLETED, MISSING_MANDATORY, MISSING_RECOMMENDED, NOT_REQUIRED)
- **Reason for Request**: Your justification for requesting access

### Linked Objects

At the bottom of the request view, you'll see three linked objects:

1. **Linked Use Case**: The AWS/Snowflake Use Case associated with this request
2. **Linked Scope**: The scope that contains the entitlement
3. **Linked Entitlement**: The specific entitlement being requested

### Pre-requisite Checks Tab (Beta)

![Pre-requisites PE View](/assets/foundry-access-management/pre-requisites-view.png)

This tab shows detailed results of prerequisite validation:

**Summary Section:**
- Total number of checks performed
- Number of passed checks
- Number of failed checks
- Mandatory checks that failed (if any)

**Individual Checks:**

Each prerequisite check displays:
- **Check Name**: Type and target of the check (e.g., TRAINING - UP_SAC, ACCOUNT - SADM)
- **Type**: Whether the prerequisite is Mandatory or Recommended
- **Status**: PASSED or FAILED with visual indicators (✅ or ❌)
- **Checked At**: Timestamp when the check was performed
- **Verification Source**: Where the data was verified from (e.g., Completed Training Object, SADM Users Object)
- **Details**: Specific information about the check (training_id, completion_date, account details, etc.)
- **Error** (if failed): Explanation of why the check failed

**Properties Panel:**

Shows the ARO Pre-Requisite Check object properties:
- Raw Check Results (JSON)
- Checked At timestamp
- Expires At (earliest expiration from all checks)
- Overall Status
- Rule Id used for validation
- Triggered By (MANUAL, AUTO_DATA_UPDATE, AUTO_SCHEDULED, AUTO_EXPIRATION)
- Triggered By User

## Getting Help

If you encounter issues:
- **granting_failed**: Contact your Use Case Owner or system administrator
- **revocation_failed**: Contact system administrator for manual intervention
- **Prerequisite questions**: Contact training administrators or account managers
- **General questions**: Reach out to your IT support team

**Last Updated**: January 2026

# Data Treasury Item (DTI) access management

![concept_access_request_DTI](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/concept_access_request_DTI.png)

**IMPORTANT CHANGE FOR DATA TREASURY ITEMS ACCESS REQEUSTS:** The access request and approval process for Data Treasury Items changed: Instead of granting access to the requesting user, **the requesting Use Case Editor Group will now be given access to the Data Treasury Item**. This means that everyone who is part of the Use Case Editor Group (use case developers) will get access to the DTI. This change has been made to improve the overall access management process and endorse the use case centric access approach. With this change, access to a DTI has to be raised only once. **Additionally, only the Use Case Owners (Product Owners, Business Owner, Technical Leads) can request access to DTIs**.

With the previous process, each developer working on a Use Case and wanting to consume data had to request access to a DTI for the same use case:

![process_change](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/process_change.png)

---

# Request Access to Data Treasury Item (DTI) 

*Please note: the user interface is under constant development, so the screenshots you see below might be changing and will get updated regularly.*
1. If you want to access a particular Data Treasury item, you can do it via the [Data Treasury](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.10e9a51d-489e-4610-b6ce-e93a1bc66912) app in the Foundry home page.
2. Once you have opened Data Treasury, you can then browse through the available Data Treasury items and select the one you want access to by clicking on the selected item. It will take you to the landing page of that DTI.
3. From here, you can click on the **'Request Permission Access'** button, which will take you to the access request form that needs to be completed to gain the required access:

# Treasurized Object Types

A <b class="custom-color">Treasurized Object Type</b> is an Object Type which is backed by a DTI Dataset. 

The access management process for DTIs starts with an Access Request raised by a member of a Use Case.

![Access Request](/assets/ontology/Access_Request_concept.png)

Upon approval there are two scenarios how the access to the Ontology data is
provided to a Use Case:

* **Data Provisioning disabled:**<br>
The Use Case Editor group is added to the Ontology Viewer group. This allows the Use Case Editors to import data as needed into the Use Case and by this providing access to that data also to Use Case Viewers.![Ontology Viewer group](/assets/ontology/Persona.png)

![Data Provisioning disabled](/assets/ontology/Person_2.png)

* **Data Provisioning enabled:**<br>
The Use Case members do not get direct access to the Ontology Project space -- not even the Editor group. Instead, the requestor specifies which data is needed for the Use Case and according to the approval, data is directly provisioned into the Use Case project space by the Data Owner.

![Data Provisioning enabled](/assets/ontology/Persona_3.png)

## Relation of an Object Type to its corresponding DTI.

A Data Treasury Item (DTI) defines an Ontology project space that contains a core dataset and a set of roles that determine the ownership for the item. This roughly outlined setup is going to be extended when creating Object Types that are backed by a dataset that is located in the DTI project space. With that a DTI will automatically be linked to the Object Types that are derived from it. 

![Relation of an Object Type to its corresponding DTI](/assets/ontology/Relation_1.png)

## Managing access to a Treasurized Object Type

Access to an Object Type is divided into the access to the underlying Object Data and the Object Metadata. While the former one is defined by the access to the backing dataset(s), the latter one is dependent on the Ontology role on the Object Type itself which can be defined in the Ontology Manager Application. 

![Managing access to a Treasurized Object Type](/assets/ontology/relation_2.png)

For DTIs, the access to the dataset is managed on the level of the ontology project space by Ontology Projects security groups i.e. Owner, Editor and Viewer multipass groups.

*	``<sector>-<ontology-project-name>-viewer``
*	``<sector>-<ontology-project-name>-editor``
*	``<sector>-<ontology-project-name>-owner``

Corresponding groups will be created for the Ontology Owner, Editor and Viewer role to manage the access for the Object Types that are derived from the given Ontology project space. The location of the backing dataset of an Object Types defines the assignment of these groups. For each Ontology project space, a set of Ontology Object security groups (multipass groups) is generated following the same pattern. 

* ``<sector>-<ontology-project-name>-ontology-objects-viewer``
* ``<sector>-<ontology-project-name>-ontology-objects-editor``
* ``<sector>-<ontology-project-name>-ontology-objects-owner``

Upon creation of an Object Type, these groups will be assigned with Ontology Owner, Editor and Viewer role, while the Ontology Owner role of the creator of the Object Type will be revoked and following DTI roles will be added to Object security editor group. 

![Managing access to a Treasurized Object Type](/assets/ontology/relation_3.png)

## DTI Roles

![DTI Roles](/assets/ontology/DTI_Roles.png)

## Management of Object Security Groups

The Ontology Object security groups will be managed by sector specific static multipass groups. In order to structure this properly for each of the above role specific Object security groups, there is a set of groups defined to assign these sector specific static groups as <b>Members</b> or with <b>Manage permissions</b> and <b>Manage membership permission</b>.

* ``<ontology-project-name>-ontology-objects-viewer``. It contains as subgroups:
  * ``<sector>-ontology-objects-viewer-member``
  * ``<sector>-ontology-objects-viewer-manage-membership``
  * ``<sector>-ontology-objects-viewer-manage-permissions``

* ``<ontology-project-name>-ontology-objects-editor``. It contains as subgroups:
  * ``<sector>-ontology-objects-editor-member``
  * ``<sector>-ontology-objects-editor-manage-membership``
  * ``<sector>-ontology-objects-editor-manage-permissions``

* ``<ontology-project-name>-ontology-objects-owner``. It contains as subgroups:
  * ``<sector>-ontology-objects-owner-member``
  * ``<sector>-ontology-objects-owner-manage-membership``
  * ``<sector>-ontology-objects-owner-manage-permissions``

<a href="/assets/ontology/Mgmt_of_Object_Security_Groups.png">![Management of Object Security Groups](/assets/ontology/Mgmt_of_Object_Security_Groups.png)</a>

Members of the Sector specific static multipass groups are defined by the SDAOs. 

<b>Important Note: For Non-Treasurized Datasets backed Object Types,</b> access will be managed with same concept (as above) of Ontology Object security groups and Sector specific static multipass groups to manage Object security groups.

Access to the Object security groups will need to be requested to the respective Sector Ontology Admins.

## Requirements for access provisioning of Treasurized Object Types 

When providing Object Types as data products to be used by multiple Use Cases it is important to manage the access in a way that allows to directly use the original Object Type(s) of the DTI within the Use Case. Otherwise Use Cases will be reindexing the very same data by creating their own copies of the very same Object Type.

This implies that not only the Use Case Editor group but also the Use Case Viewer group must get access to the dataset which is backing the Object Type(s). This is realized by adding those groups to the Viewer group of the Ontology project of a given DTI. In addition, the Use Case Editors and Viewers must receive access to the Object Type itself. This is achieved by adding the Use Case Editor and Viewer groups to the Ontology project specific Object group Viewer. 

The Use Case will then be able to consume the original Object Type in an Ontology-aware application (like Workshop).

![Requirements for access provisioning of Treasurized Object Types](/assets/ontology/access_provisioning_of_Treasurized.png)

Any data that is not aimed at being provided to particular Use Cases must be secured by using restricted views. The dataset that is backing the restricted view can either be protected by locating it in a separate project or by applying a marking.

![Requirements for access provisioning of Treasurized Object Types-2](/assets/ontology/access_provisioning_of_Treasurized_2.png)

## Access to Link Type where a Use case driven Object Type has created a link to Ontology Project driven Object Type

In case where a Use case driven Object Type has created a link to Ontology Project driven Object Type, the Link Type will be co-owned by Use Case & DTI Owner. Such Link types will be assigned all Use Case groups (Use Case Owner, Editor, Viewer) as well as Object Security Owner and Editor groups. Any user groups having access to Link type will be kept intact while revoking specific user access.

![Use case driven Object Type has created a link to Ontology Project driven Object Type](/assets/ontology/Use_case_driven_Object_Type.png)

---

# Access Management Process for Treasurized Object Types

## Introduction

**What is a Treasurized Object Type?**

It is an Object Type which is backed by a DTI Dataset. 

To establish a better governance around Treasurized Object Types Access (Object Types backed by DTI Dataset) and further improve the user experience on the platform, we have enhanced the DTI access management process to include the following key capabilities: 

* Access request process for Treasurized Object Types
* Instead of individual user, now Use Case Editor and Viewer will have access to Treasurized Object Types. 
* Temporary Access for Treasurized Object Types which follows the expiration date set for DTI Access. 

Furthermore, this change enables the re-use of the Object Type itself for various Use cases by providing Use Case Editor and Viewer Groups Viewer access to the DTI and Treasurized Object Types instead of a need for making copies of the Object Type in the Use Case project space. 

Please also see the document [Access Concept for Treasurized Object Types](foundry/foundry-access-management/dti/Access-Concept-for-Treasurized-Object-Types/request-access/) to learn more about the Overall Access Concept. 

**Important Change for Data Treasury Items Access Requests:** 

The access request and approval process for Data Treasury Items (DTI) has been enhanced: Now along with the DTI access, the Treasurized Object Type access can also be requested for the Use Case projects. As a result of this process, the requesting Use Case Editor Group and Use Case Viewer Group will now be given access to the DTI and Treasurized Object Types thereby driving the re-use of the Object Type itself instead of a need for making copies of the Object Type in the Use Case project space. This means that everyone who is part of the Use Case Editor Group (use case developers) and Use Case Viewer Group (consumers) will get access to the DTI and Treasurized Object Types.  

Only the Use Case Owners (Product Owners, Business Owner, Technical Leads) can request access to DTIs and Treasurized Object Types. 


##  Access Requests for Treasurized Object Types along with DTI access.

![Concept 1: Access Requests for Treasurized Object Types along with DTI access](/assets/ontology/Concept-1.png)

The above concept gives a detailed understanding of how the user can raise a request for Treasurized Object Types along with the DTI access request. 

The above schematic shows the Object Type access process along with DTI access request. The requester will have the option to select which DTI the Use Case needs access to. Once the DTI is selected, they will have options to select a Use Case from the dropdown, allowing the user to request access to the DTI & Treasurized Object Types. 

After selecting the Use Case project(s), the user should choose the -editor and -viewer groups associated with the use case project(s). Once the request is approved, both the Use Case editor and viewer groups will gain access to the DTI & Treasurized Object Types. 

![Object Type access along with DTI access request](/assets/ontology/Concept-1_image.png)

Example of Object Type access along with DTI access request. 

## Access for Treasurized Object Types for Use Cases already having DTI access.

![Access Requests for Treasurized Object Types for the Use Cases already having DTI access](/assets/ontology/Concept-2.png)

The above concept gives a detailed understanding of how the user can raise a request for Treasurized Object Types for the Use Cases already having DTI access. 

The above schematic displays Treasurized Object Types access request process when the Use Case is already having DTI access. The requester will have the option to select which DTI the Use Case needs access to. Once the DTI is selected, the linked Use Cases and Use Case projects already having access to the DTI will be listed in a dropdown menu, allowing the user to select the Use Case and Use Case project(s) next. 

After selecting the Use Case project(s), the user should choose the -editor and -viewer groups associated with the Use Case project(s). Once the request is approved, both the Use Case editor and viewer groups will gain access to the Treasurized Object Types. 

![Treasurized Object Types access when the Use Case is already having DTI access](/assets/ontology/Concept-2_Image.png)

Example of Treasurized Object Types access when the Use Case is already having DTI access. 

**Request Access: Treasurized Object Types.** 

If you want to access a DTI, you can do it via the Data Treasury app in the Foundry home page. 

Once you have opened Data Treasury, you can then browse through the available Data Treasury Items and select the one a Use Case needs access to by clicking on the selected item. It will take you to the landing page of that DTI. 

From here, you can click on the 'Request Access to DTI and Object Type(s)' button, which will take you to the access request form that needs to be completed to gain the required access: 

![Request Access: Treasurized Object Types](/assets/ontology/Request_Access_Treasurized_Object_Types.png)

**Access Requests for Treasurized object types along with DTI access:**

* Once you have selected the DTI to which access is needed, you will see the DTI project and DTI viewer group (Ontology Project Security group) to which Use Case group will be added to.

![Access Requests for Treasurized object types along with DTI access](/assets/ontology/Access_Request_details.png)

* As a next step, you must select the Use Case which should get access to the Data Treasury Item.

* Once you have selected the Use Case, you can specify the Use Case project which should get access to the Data Treasury Item.

* Once the project is selected, the -editor group of this project will automatically be pre-selected.

 * <b>Note:</b> Only the editor group of the Use Case will get access to the Data Treasury Item. You cannot select the viewer group. 

![Use Case Details](/assets/ontology/Use_Case_Details.png)

 If Object Type(s) exist related to selected DTI, as a next step, you will have a question that says, 'Do you need access to Object Types related to above DTI?'.

* If yes, you must 'Select all' the Object Types that are related to the DTI (Reason: since the Object Type access is controlled at the DTI Project level, access to any one Object Type would anyways provide access to all Object Types).

* Based on the DTI selected earlier in the form, you will see the pre-selected Object Viewer group (Ontology Object Security group) and DTI Viewer group (Ontology Project Security group) to which Use Case editor and viewer groups will be added.

* Based on the Use Case Project(s) selected earlier in the form, please select the Use Case project editor and viewer groups which should get access to the Treasurized Object Types.

* <b>Note:</b> Both the -editor and -viewer group of the selected Use Case Projects must be selected so that both groups get access to the Treasurized Object Types. 

![Object Types & Target Groups](/assets/ontology/Object_Type_&_Target_Group.png)

* It is important that a valid reason is provided why you need access to the specific Use Case.

* If you need access only for a certain period, you can set an expiration date of your access request. After the expiration date, the access to the DTI and Object Type will automatically be revoked.

![Reason for this request](/assets/ontology/Reason_for_request.png)

**Access Requests for Treasurized object types for the use case that already have DTI access:**

* Once you have selected the DTI to which access is needed, you will see the DTI project and DTI viewer group (Ontology Project Security group) to which Use Case groups will be added to.

![Access Requests for Treasurized object types for the use case that already have DTI access](/assets/ontology/Access_Request_Details_2.png)

* As a next step, you must 'Select all' the Object Types that are related to the DTI (Reason: since the Object Type access is controlled at the DTI Project level, access to any one Object Type would anyway provide access to all Object Types).

* Based on the DTI selected earlier in the form, you will see the Object Viewer group (Ontology Object Security group) to which Use Case editor and viewer groups will be added. 

![Select Object Types & Target Group](/assets/ontology/Object_Type_&_Target_Group_2.png)

* As a next step, you must select the Use Case which needs access to the Object Type(s) from the dropdown. Only the Use Cases(s) already having access to DTI selected earlier in the form are displayed in dropdown.

* Once you have selected the Use Case, you can select the Use Case project which should get access to the Object Type(s) from the dropdown. Only the Use Case projects that have an approved DTI access request are available in the dropdown. In case a Use Case project is not available in the dropdown, please raise a DTI access request for that Use Case project first and get it approved.

Based on the selected Use Case Project(s), please select the Use Case project editor and viewer groups which should get access to the Treasurized Object Types.

* <b> Note:</b> Both the -editor and -viewer group of the selected Use Case Projects must be selected so that both groups get access to the Treasurized Object Types. 

![Use Case Details](/assets/ontology/Use_case_details_2.png)

* It is important that a valid reason is provided why you need access to the specific Use Case.

![Reason for this request](/assets/ontology/Reason_for_request_2.png)

**Treasurized Object Type Access Requests:**

* Navigate to the User Access Management application. You will find the access requests you can Approve or Reject under the tab "Manage access requests".

* This will show you the access requests you have to manage by either Approving or Rejecting them.

* By default, the list will show all open access requests. If you want to see your previously raised access requests, click on "All" under the tab "My access requests". 

**Approve Action:** 

The approval workflows for DTI access and Object Type access are handled separately. The "Approve" button for Object Type access will only be visible to the approver once the DTI access request is approved. The approver has the authority and responsibility to also approve the Object Type access request. 

**Reject Action:**

DTI and Object Type access requests can be rejected together if the approver decides to reject both using "Reject DTI & Object Access Request" button. DTI access request cannot be rejected independently if it has associated Object Type access request. However, Object Type access requests can be rejected independently using the button "Reject Object Type Access Request". If the Object Type access request is rejected already, DTI Access request can then be rejected using the button "Reject DTI Access Request".  
 
**Revoke Action:** 

Approver can revoke both DTI and Object Type access using the button "Revoke" in case both the access requests have been granted. In case, Object Type access request is pending, revocation of granted DTI Access will reject the related Object Type access request. 

**Edit Action:** 

When the request status is pending, the approvers can edit both DTI and Object Type access requests separately using the "Edit" buttons. 
 
**Make Permanent Action:** 

Once access is granted, if the approvers decide to make the access permanent, they can make both the DTI and Object Type access permanent using the "Make Access Permanent" button. 
 
**Withdraw Action:** 

When the status is pending, the requester could withdraw both the DTI and Object Type access requests together using the "Withdraw DTI & Object Type Access Request" button or only the Object Type access request (using the "Withdraw Object Type Access Request" button). If only the Object Type access request is withdrawn, DTI access request can be withdrawn using "Withdraw" button.

---

# Data source and transform access management

In general, data source and transform projects are managed by the SDAOs. This means, that for the project with project name ``<project-name>``, the standard groups

* ``<sector>-<project-name>-ontology-objects-viewer``
* ``<sector>-<project-name>-ontology-objects-editor``
* ``<sector>-<project-name>-ontology-objects-owner``

will contain the respective sector wrapper groups.
