# SAP-to-Snowflake Automated Data Validation

## What is this?

This project is an **automated data validation tool** that ensures data replicated from SAP into Snowflake arrives **complete and unchanged**. It answers a simple question:

> *"Is what we see in Snowflake the same as what exists in SAP?"*

The process takes place inside Palantir Foundry and performs three checks per table:

- **Schema check** -- Are the column names and data types consistent between the two systems?
- **Row count check** -- Does Snowflake contain the same number of records as SAP?
- **Sample row check** -- Can we find a representative sample of SAP rows in Snowflake, value by value?

Results are collected into a single dataset so teams can monitor data integrity at a glance.

## Why does this exist?

Data moves from SAP to Snowflake through a multi-step replication pipeline (HVR / CDC). Along the way, records can be dropped, columns can shift types, or replication lag can cause counts to drift. These discrepancies are often silent -- nothing fails, the data just quietly diverges.

This tool makes those gaps visible and measurable.

## Current scope (POC)

The current implementation is a **proof of concept** targeting **SAP P70** as the source system. A small set of tables (AFPO, EKET, LIPS) has been configured to validate the approach end-to-end. P70 was chosen as the first candidate, but the design is not specific to it.

**The underlaying Oracle JDBC Foundry extract objects are meant to run once a month not to cause the SAP source to be overflowed with work.**

## Where this is heading

The architecture is intentionally generic. To onboard a new SAP source system, the main things that change are:

- The Oracle connection / schema name
- The list of tables and their Virtual Table RIDs in Snowflake
- The batch configuration entries

The comparison engine, type mapping, result aggregation, and reporting layer stay the same. The goal is for this to scale across SAP source systems so that any table being replicated into Snowflake can be continuously validated with minimal setup.

---

# Foundry Glossary

| Term                                   | Definition                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
|----------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Action Type                            | An action type is the schema definition of a set of changes or edits to objects,property values, and links that a user can take at once.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Application Portal                     | Applications Portal is a tool for finding and accessing all apps in Foundry, including both platform apps and custom promoted applications.                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Branch                                 | Branch on the Ontology is a separate version of that Ontology, derived from the main version, designed to enable experimentation and  changes without impacting the main branch.                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Build                                  | A Build is the mechanism used to compute new versions of datasets in Foundry. Builds provide orchestration and coordination of computation, ensure the appropriate input data is read, and write output data to the appropriate location                                                                                                                                  |
| Carbon Workspace                       | Application builders in Foundry can use Carbon to create curated, custom workspaces for their end users. A wide range of applications can be combined together to provide a tailored experience.                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Code repository                        | Enhance object ontology functions & relations e.g. for use  in workshop dashboards (in TypeScript).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Contour                                | User friendly, intuitive point & click tool for quick top-down analysis of large data.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Data Connection                        | App to ingest data to the data lake.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Data Enhancement Request (DER)         | A data enhancement request refers to a formal process or a request made to improve the quality, completeness, or accuracy of a dataset. It involves enhancing the existing data by adding additional information, refining existing data points, or correcting errors.                                                                                                    |
| Data Health                            | Monitor and configure robust alerting for datasets and builds.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |	
| Data Provisioning                      | Data Provisioning is a process that allows the owner of a  Data Treasury Item to granularly control which subset of the data a Use Case has access to.                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Data Lineage                           | Every dataset in Foundry maintains a record of how it was produced, so that the origins of data are always preserved and accessible. This concept is known as data lineage.                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Data Treasury                          | One-stop-shop for browsing, discovering and accessing data within the Merck organization to build your Use Case on UPTIMIZE Foundry.It has been designed to optimize searchability, auditability and  discoverability of data as well as incorporating and enforcing core data governance workflows.                                                                      |
| Dataset                                | A dataset is a set or collection of data.	                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Datasource derived permissions         | Datasource derived permissions are the legacy solution for authorizing Ontology resources. Datasource derived permissions rely on the permissions defined on the backing datasource for each object type, creating a direct 1:1 dependency between object types in the Ontology and the backing datasource.	                                                             |
| Decommissioned                         | The POV or Industrialized Use Case has been discontinued and is no longer being developed or supported.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| Deferred (On Hold)                     | In this stage stakeholders are waiting for additional support or information before revisiting the Use Case development.	                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Data Ingestion Request (DIR)           | A Data Ingestion Request is a formal process or request made to bring external data into a system or platform for processing, analysis, or storage.                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Discarded                              | Ideas that we will likely not come back to, or Use Cases that are duplicates and no longer needed.	                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Favorites                              | The Favorites section of the sidebar keeps links to specific apps, resources, and individual objects for quick navigation.	                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Files                                  | Projects & files links to the landing page for the Project folder structure, where you can access top-level Projects and the Data Catalog, Your files, and Shared with you shortcuts.	                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| Hubble / object explorer               | Hubble / object explorer:Point and click solution to explore your data objects and relations between them through interactive charts.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Industrialization                      | The Use Case POV has been successful and so the outputs are being continually developed, supported and rolled out to the target user base.	                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Link Type                              | A link type is the schema definition of a relationship between two object types. A link refers to a single instance of that relationship between two objects in  the same Ontology.	                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Markings                               | Markings are used to add an additional layer of permission management to resources. No matter what access rights a user has, as long as a file is flags with a Marking the user does not have, the use can not see or access the file.                                                                                                                                    |
| Notifications                          | The Notifications panel collects notices from across the platform, ordered from newest to oldest. Most notifications include links to navigate directly to the  relevant resources. Some, such as access requests	                                                                                                                                                       |
| Object Type                            | An object type is the semantic representation of the entity itself (such as the name and properties of the object).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Ontology                               | The Foundry Ontology is an operational layer for the organization.The Ontology sits on top of the digital assets integrated into Foundry <br>(datasets and models) and connects them to their real-world counterparts, ranging from physical assets like plants, equipment,<br> and products to concepts like customer orders or financial transactions.                  |	
| Ontology Discoverer                    | Can only see Ontology resource name and metadata, excluding schema.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Ontology Editor                        | Can edit Ontology resources.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Ontology Index                         | Foundry's Ontology stores objects in an Ontology index, a storage format optimized for rapid access. Data in Foundry datasets can be of any size or format, meaning a data transformation is required to prepare dataset data for storage in an Ontology index. This process is known as Ontology indexing and can be applied to datasets and objects of arbitrary size.  |
| Ontology Manager                       | Create and manage Objects, their properties, security and datasources.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Ontology Owner                         | Can edit Ontology resources and has full control over their security and sharing.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Ontology Proposals                     | Ontology proposals allow you to make changes to an Ontology on a branch, which is based on the main version of that Ontology.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |	
| Ontology Roles                         | Ontology roles are the new and improved solution for authorizing Ontology resources, and will be the default authorization model.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Ontology Viewer                        | Can view Ontology resources, but cannot edit them.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Ontology Volume                        | Ontology volume is a measure of the total size of the indexed object sets and their links with each other. Ontology volume is an average metric that has the unit of GB for an instantaneous reading, but has the unit of GB-Month when measuring over the course of one month.                                                                                           |
| Pipeline Builder                       | Point & click tool for building data integration pipelines from data sources through to final outputs.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Planning                               | Stakeholders are aligning and gathering information on how to implement the Use Case and how it will be measured.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Projects                               | Resources are organized into Projects, which serve as permission boundaries for grouping and organizing related work.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   	 |
| Proof of Value <br>Development (POV)   | The first version of the Use Case is being developed and built.At the end of the initial Proof of Value (POV) implementation, <br>the Use Case will be assessed for whether it will be continued or decommissioned.In this status, a project folder will be automatically created for and linked to your Use Case.                                                        |	
| Proposal                               | A proposal is analogous to a Pull Request in a version control system, specifically tailored for Ontology branches. A proposal is automatically created along side a branch and contains metadata such as reviews, name, and descriptions of the changes being merged into the main branch.                                                                               |	
| Quiver                                 | Visualize, analyze, and transform Foundry-backed objects and time series at scale.	                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Recent                                 | The Recent panel simply lists the last 20 resources you've opened or interacted with. Between Favorites and Recent, it's possible to quickly navigate between primary resources in use for any project without needing to return to Search or browse through the Project folder structure.	                                                                               |
| Reports                                | Point & click tool for quick top-down analysis of insights & simple visualizations.	                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Resource                               | When you use applications, anything you produce, whether it's a dataset, code, or analysis, is stored in Foundry as a resource.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Scheduler                              | Enables you to set up scheduled builds of your data pipelines in order to ensure that your data stays up-to-date.	                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Semi-structured Dataset                | Semi-structured datasets contain file formats such as XML or JSON. While it's possible to apply schemas to these file formats.	                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Serach                                 | Search in Foundry, also known as Quicksearch, is a tool for navigation and discovery.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |	
| Shared Ontology                        | A shared ontology is a special kind of ontology that allows multiple Organizations to collaborate on shared workflows. Shared ontologies live under a  dedicated shared namespace created specifically for the workflow.	                                                                                                                                                 |
| Slate                                  | Build elaborate sophisticated apps that query and analyze data with drag-and-drop visualization and input widgets to drive business workflows.                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Structured Dataset                     | Structured (tabular) data consists of files that contain tabular data in an open source format such as Parquet, along with metadata about the columns in the dataset.                                                                                                                                                                                                     |	
| User Access Management                 | User access management refers to the process of controlling and managing user permissions and access rights within the Foundry platform.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Use Case                               | A use case is a time-bound effort by a dedicated team to deliver new capabilities on the platform for a set of users.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Use Case Portal                        | The Use Case Portal is the one-stop-shop for tracking work in UPTIMIZE across the global Merck Organization. Start exploring existing Use Cases by Business Sector, create a new Use Case or request access to an existing one.                                                                                                                                           |
| Unstructured Dataset                   | Unstructured datasets consist of files such as images, video, or PDFs, but do not have an associated schema.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Workshop                               | Create high-quality, easy-to-maintain operational applications using native object components in a point-and-click environment.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         	 |

---

## Introduction

Any Foundry user can now raise a request to become a member of the supported sector-specific Admin/Capability groups by submitting a Use Case access request for the following sector-specific use case:
- EF Admin Group Management - Use case for EF sector
- HC Admin Group Management - Use Case for Healthcare sector
- EL Admin Group Management - Use Case for Electronics sector
- ACE Admin Group Management - Use Case for Life Science sector
- MDAO  Admin Group Management - Use Case for MDAO

|  |**Use Case Access Requests Form:**
|:---------|:---------------|
![access_request_1](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/access_request_1.png) | - You can either access via the [User Access Management](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.60d62422-3f90-4bfb-8b5e-b33a4ccd966e) or the [Use Case Portal](https://palantir.mcloud.merckgroup.com/workspace/module/view/latest/ri.workshop.main.module.cfbd54d9-5f5e-4c67-a94d-37fc842812cc)<br><br>

## Steps to follow -
1.	In Use Case Portal 2.0, select your sector specific Use Case from above mentioned list.
2.	Click on "Request Access to Use case" button -
 ![use_case_access_request](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/use-case-access-request.png)
3.	Select the User requesting access.
4.	Select the Admin/Capability Group from the "Preset" dropdown.
![use_case_access_request](https://docs.uptimize.merckgroup.com/docs-assets/foundry/Images/user_access_management/use-case-access-request-form.png) 
5.	Provide a proper reason for this request so that approver can validate the request.
6.	If you need access only for a certain period, you can set an expiration date of your access request 
7.	Click on the "Submit" button.
Once the request is submitted, an automated email will be sent to the approvers, and the selected user will be automatically added as a member of the admin group upon approval.
